  979 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      2 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0652               | * Create_Sprite — Compiled sprite engine
  980 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      3 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0652               | * Ported from FTA's CREATE.SPRITE.S (1989)
  981 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      4 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0652               | *
  982 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      5 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0652               | * Compiles shape data into native 65816 code that
  983 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      6 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0652               | * draws sprites via direct-page writes to SHR shadow RAM.
  984 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      7 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0652               | *
  985 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      8 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0652               | * Call: copy sprite table ($18 bytes) to bank $00 direct page,
  986 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      9 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0652               | *       LDA #dp_address / JSR Create_Sprite
  987 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     10 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0652               | *
  988 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     11 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0652               | * Sprite table format (24 bytes at DP offsets $00-$17):
  989 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     12 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0652               | *   $00 ADRL Rout_Adr    — output: where compiled code is written
  990 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     13 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0652               | *   $04 ADRL Shape_Adr   — input: shape pixel data (24-bit)
  991 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     14 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0652               | *   $08 ADRL Msk_Adr     — $000000=none, $FFFF00=auto, $FEFE00=decor
  992 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     15 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0652               | *   $0C DA   Tbl_Nb      — TABLE_ROUT index (updated by routine)
  993 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     16 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0652               | *   $0E DA   Nb_Lgn      — bytes per shape row
  994 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     17 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0652               | *   $10 DA   Nb_Col      — bytes per shape column
  995 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     18 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0652               | *   $12 DA   Lgn         — row ($FFFF=dynamic via Y register)
  996 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     19 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0652               | *   $14 DA   Col         — column
  997 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     20 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0652               | *   $16 DA   Pixel_Shape — $00=no sub-pixel, $01=half-pixel shift
  998 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     21 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0652               | *-------------------------------------------------
